I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[cmd/opampsupervisor] Reload Collector configuration with SIGHUP
### Component(s)

cmd/opampsupervisor

### Is your feature request related to a problem? Please describe.

Currently the Supervisor restarts the Collector by stop its process and starting again. 

### Describe the solution you'd like

I would like the Supervisor to use [the SIGHUP configuration reload feature baked in the Collector](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector/pull/6000) to delegate the configuration reload work to the Collector itself.



### Describe alternatives you've considered

- Use an HTTP endpoint to trigger the configuration reload on the Collector: not possible until https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector/issues/10264 is completed.
- Hot reload of configuration: just not ready yet, as discussed in https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector/issues/5966.

### Additional context

_No response_

</pr_description>

     1	// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
     2	// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

     4	package commander
     5	
     6	import (
     7	        "bufio"
     8	        "context"
     9	        "errors"
    10	        "fmt"
    11	        "os"
    12	        "os/exec"
    13	        "path/filepath"
    14	        "slices"
    15	        "sync/atomic"
    16	        "time"
    17	
    18	        "go.uber.org/zap"
    19	
    20	        "github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector-contrib/cmd/opampsupervisor/supervisor/common"
    21	        "github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector-contrib/cmd/opampsupervisor/supervisor/config"
    22	)
    23	
    24	// Commander can start/stop/restart the Agent executable and also watch for a signal
    25	// for the Agent process to finish.
    26	type Commander struct {
    27	        logger  *zap.Logger
    28	        cfg     config.Agent
    29	        logsDir string
    30	        args    []string
    31	        cmd     *exec.Cmd
    32	        doneCh  chan struct{}
    33	        exitCh  chan struct{}
    34	        running *atomic.Int64
    35	}
    36	
    37	func NewCommander(logger *zap.Logger, logsDir string, cfg config.Agent, args ...string) (*Commander, error) {
    38	        return &Commander{
    39	                logger:  logger,
    40	                logsDir: logsDir,
    41	                cfg:     cfg,
    42	                args:    args,
    43	                running: &atomic.Int64{},
    44	                // Buffer channels so we can send messages without blocking on listeners.
    45	                doneCh: make(chan struct{}, 1),
    46	                exitCh: make(chan struct{}, 1),
    47	        }, nil
    48	}
    49	
    50	// Start the Agent and begin watching the process.
    51	// Agent's stdout and stderr are written to a file.
    52	// Calling this method when a command is already running
    53	// is a no-op.
    54	func (c *Commander) Start(ctx context.Context) error {
    55	        if c.running.Load() == 1 {
    56	                // Already started, nothing to do
    57	                return nil
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        // Drain channels in case there are no listeners that
    61	        // drained messages from previous runs.
    62	        if len(c.doneCh) > 0 {
    63	                select {
    64	                case <-c.doneCh:
    65	                default:
    66	                }
    67	        }
    68	        if len(c.exitCh) > 0 {
    69	                select {
    70	                case <-c.exitCh:
    71	                default:
    72	                }
    73	        }
    74	        c.logger.Debug("Starting agent", zap.String("agent", c.cfg.Executable))
    75	
    76	        args := slices.Concat(c.args, c.cfg.Arguments)
    77	
    78	        c.cmd = exec.CommandContext(ctx, c.cfg.Executable, args...) // #nosec G204
    79	        c.cmd.Env = common.EnvVarMapToEnvMapSlice(c.cfg.Env)
    80	        c.cmd.SysProcAttr = sysProcAttrs()
    81	
    82	        // PassthroughLogging changes how collector start up happens
    83	        if c.cfg.PassthroughLogs {
    84	                return c.startWithPassthroughLogging()
    85	        }
    86	        return c.startNormal()
    87	}
    88	
    89	func (c *Commander) Restart(ctx context.Context) error {
    90	        c.logger.Debug("Restarting agent", zap.String("agent", c.cfg.Executable))
    91	        if err := c.Stop(ctx); err != nil {
    92	                return err
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        return c.Start(ctx)
    96	}
    97	
    98	func (c *Commander) startNormal() error {
    99	        logFilePath := filepath.Join(c.logsDir, "agent.log")
   100	        stdoutFile, err := os.Create(logFilePath)
   101	        if err != nil {
   102	                return fmt.Errorf("cannot create %s: %w", logFilePath, err)
   103	        }
   104	
   105	        // Capture standard output and standard error.
   106	        // https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector-contrib/issues/21072
   107	        c.cmd.Stdout = stdoutFile
   108	        c.cmd.Stderr = stdoutFile
   109	
   110	        if err := c.cmd.Start(); err != nil {
   111	                stdoutFile.Close()
   112	                return fmt.Errorf("startNormal: %w", err)
   113	        }
   114	
   115	        c.logger.Debug("Agent process started", zap.Int("pid", c.cmd.Process.Pid))
   116	        c.running.Store(1)
   117	
   118	        go func() {
   119	                defer stdoutFile.Close()
   120	                c.watch()
   121	        }()
   122	
   123	        return nil
   124	}
   125	
   126	func (c *Commander) startWithPassthroughLogging() error {
   127	        // grab cmd pipes
   128	        stdoutPipe, err := c.cmd.StdoutPipe()
   129	        if err != nil {
   130	                return fmt.Errorf("stdoutPipe: %w", err)
   131	        }
   132	        stderrPipe, err := c.cmd.StderrPipe()
   133	        if err != nil {
   134	                return fmt.Errorf("stderrPipe: %w", err)
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        // start agent
   138	        if err := c.cmd.Start(); err != nil {
   139	                return fmt.Errorf("start: %w", err)
   140	        }
   141	        c.running.Store(1)
   142	
   143	        colLogger := c.logger.Named("collector")
   144	
   145	        // capture agent output
   146	        go func() {
   147	                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stdoutPipe)
   148	                for scanner.Scan() {
   149	                        line := scanner.Text()
   150	                        colLogger.Info(line)
   151	                }
   152	                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
   153	                        c.logger.Error("Error reading agent stdout: %w", zap.Error(err))
   154	                }
   155	        }()
   156	        go func() {
   157	                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stderrPipe)
   158	                for scanner.Scan() {
   159	                        line := scanner.Text()
   160	                        colLogger.Error(line)
   161	                }
   162	                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
   163	                        c.logger.Error("Error reading agent stderr: %w", zap.Error(err))
   164	                }
   165	        }()
   166	
   167	        c.logger.Debug("Agent process started", zap.Int("pid", c.cmd.Process.Pid))
   168	
   169	        go c.watch()
   170	        return nil
   171	}
   172	
   173	func (c *Commander) watch() {
   174	        err := c.cmd.Wait()
   175	
   176	        // cmd.Wait returns an exec.ExitError when the Collector exits unsuccessfully or stops
   177	        // after receiving a signal. The Commander caller will handle these cases, so we filter
   178	        // them out here.
   179	        var exitError *exec.ExitError
   180	        if ok := errors.As(err, &exitError); err != nil && !ok {
   181	                c.logger.Error("An error occurred while watching the agent process", zap.Error(err))
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        c.running.Store(0)
   185	        c.doneCh <- struct{}{}
   186	        c.exitCh <- struct{}{}
   187	}
   188	
   189	// StartOneShot starts the Collector with the expectation that it will immediately
   190	// exit after it finishes a quick operation. This is useful for situations like reading stdout/sterr
   191	// to e.g. check the feature gate the Collector supports.
   192	func (c *Commander) StartOneShot() ([]byte, []byte, error) {
   193	        stdout := []byte{}
   194	        stderr := []byte{}
   195	        ctx := context.Background()
   196	
   197	        cmd := exec.CommandContext(ctx, c.cfg.Executable, c.args...) // #nosec G204
   198	        cmd.Env = common.EnvVarMapToEnvMapSlice(c.cfg.Env)
   199	        cmd.SysProcAttr = sysProcAttrs()
   200	        // grab cmd pipes
   201	        stdoutPipe, err := cmd.StdoutPipe()
   202	        if err != nil {
   203	                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("stdoutPipe: %w", err)
   204	        }
   205	        stderrPipe, err := cmd.StderrPipe()
   206	        if err != nil {
   207	                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("stderrPipe: %w", err)
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        // start agent
   211	        if err := cmd.Start(); err != nil {
   212	                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("start: %w", err)
   213	        }
   214	        // capture agent output
   215	        go func() {
   216	                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stdoutPipe)
   217	                for scanner.Scan() {
   218	                        stdout = append(stdout, scanner.Bytes()...)
   219	                        stdout = append(stdout, byte('\n'))
   220	                }
   221	                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
   222	                        c.logger.Error("Error reading agent stdout: %w", zap.Error(err))
   223	                }
   224	        }()
   225	        go func() {
   226	                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stderrPipe)
   227	                for scanner.Scan() {
   228	                        stderr = append(stderr, scanner.Bytes()...)
   229	                        stderr = append(stderr, byte('\n'))
   230	                }
   231	                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
   232	                        c.logger.Error("Error reading agent stderr: %w", zap.Error(err))
   233	                }
   234	        }()
   235	
   236	        c.logger.Debug("Agent process started", zap.Int("pid", cmd.Process.Pid))
   237	
   238	        doneCh := make(chan struct{}, 1)
   239	
   240	        go func() {
   241	                err := cmd.Wait()
   242	                if err != nil {
   243	                        c.logger.Error("One-shot Collector encountered an error during execution", zap.Error(err))
   244	                }
   245	                doneCh <- struct{}{}
   246	        }()
   247	
   248	        waitCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 3*time.Second)
   249	
   250	        defer cancel()
   251	
   252	        select {
   253	        case <-doneCh:
   254	        case <-waitCtx.Done():
   255	                pid := cmd.Process.Pid
   256	                c.logger.Debug("Stopping agent process", zap.Int("pid", pid))
   257	
   258	                // Gracefully signal process to stop.
   259	                if err := sendShutdownSignal(cmd.Process); err != nil {
   260	                        return nil, nil, err
   261	                }
   262	
   263	                innerWaitCtx, innerCancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 10*time.Second)
   264	
   265	                // Setup a goroutine to wait a while for process to finish and send kill signal
   266	                // to the process if it doesn't finish.
   267	                var innerErr error
   268	                go func() {
   269	                        <-innerWaitCtx.Done()
   270	
   271	                        if !errors.Is(innerWaitCtx.Err(), context.DeadlineExceeded) {
   272	                                c.logger.Debug("Agent process successfully stopped.", zap.Int("pid", pid))
   273	                                return
   274	                        }
   275	
   276	                        // Time is out. Kill the process.
   277	                        c.logger.Debug(
   278	                                "Agent process is not responding to SIGTERM. Sending SIGKILL to kill forcibly.",
   279	                                zap.Int("pid", pid))
   280	                        if innerErr = cmd.Process.Signal(os.Kill); innerErr != nil {
   281	                                return
   282	                        }
   283	                }()
   284	
   285	                innerCancel()
   286	        }
   287	
   288	        return stdout, stderr, nil
   289	}
   290	
   291	// Exited returns a channel that will send a signal when the Agent process exits.
   292	func (c *Commander) Exited() <-chan struct{} {
   293	        return c.exitCh
   294	}
   295	
   296	// Pid returns Agent process PID if it is started or 0 if it is not.
   297	func (c *Commander) Pid() int {
   298	        if c.cmd == nil || c.cmd.Process == nil {
   299	                return 0
   300	        }
   301	        return c.cmd.Process.Pid
   302	}
   303	
   304	// ExitCode returns Agent process exit code if it exited or 0 if it is not.
   305	func (c *Commander) ExitCode() int {
   306	        if c.cmd == nil || c.cmd.ProcessState == nil {
   307	                return 0
   308	        }
   309	        return c.cmd.ProcessState.ExitCode()
   310	}
   311	
   312	func (c *Commander) IsRunning() bool {
   313	        return c.running.Load() != 0
   314	}
   315	
   316	// Stop the Agent process. Sends SIGTERM to the process and wait for up 10 seconds
   317	// and if the process does not finish kills it forcedly by sending SIGKILL.
   318	// Returns after the process is terminated.
   319	func (c *Commander) Stop(ctx context.Context) error {
   320	        if c.running.Load() == 0 {
   321	                // Not started, nothing to do.
   322	                return nil
   323	        }
   324	
   325	        pid := c.cmd.Process.Pid
   326	        c.logger.Debug("Stopping agent process", zap.Int("pid", pid))
   327	
   328	        // Gracefully signal process to stop.
   329	        if err := sendShutdownSignal(c.cmd.Process); err != nil {
   330	                return err
   331	        }
   332	
   333	        waitCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 10*time.Second)
   334	
   335	        // Setup a goroutine to wait a while for process to finish and send kill signal
   336	        // to the process if it doesn't finish.
   337	        var innerErr error
   338	        go func() {
   339	                <-waitCtx.Done()
   340	
   341	                if !errors.Is(waitCtx.Err(), context.DeadlineExceeded) {
   342	                        c.logger.Debug("Agent process successfully stopped.", zap.Int("pid", pid))
   343	                        return
   344	                }
   345	
   346	                // Time is out. Kill the process.
   347	                c.logger.Debug(
   348	                        "Agent process is not responding to SIGTERM. Sending SIGKILL to kill forcibly.",
   349	                        zap.Int("pid", pid))
   350	                if innerErr = c.cmd.Process.Signal(os.Kill); innerErr != nil {
   351	                        return
   352	                }
   353	        }()
   354	
   355	        // Wait for process to terminate
   356	        <-c.doneCh
   357	
   358	        c.running.Store(0)
   359	
   360	        // Let goroutine know process is finished.
   361	        cancel()
   362	
   363	        return innerErr
   364	}

     8	import (

    13	func sendShutdownSignal(process *os.Process) error {
    14	        return process.Signal(os.Interrupt)
    15	}

     1	// Copyright The OpenTelemetry Authors
     2	// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
     3	
     4	//go:build windows
     5	
     6	package commander
     7	
     8	import (
     9	        "fmt"
    10	        "os"
    11	        "syscall"
    12	
    13	        "golang.org/x/sys/windows"
    14	)
    15	
    16	var (
    17	        kernel32API = windows.NewLazySystemDLL("kernel32.dll")
    18	
    19	        ctrlEventProc = kernel32API.NewProc("GenerateConsoleCtrlEvent")
    20	)
    21	
    22	func sendShutdownSignal(process *os.Process) error {
    23	        // signaling with os.Interrupt is not supported on windows systems,
    24	        // so we need to use the windows API to properly send a graceful shutdown signal.
    25	        // See: https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/console/generateconsolectrlevent
    26	        r, _, e := ctrlEventProc.Call(syscall.CTRL_BREAK_EVENT, uintptr(process.Pid))
    27	        if r == 0 {
    28	                return fmt.Errorf("sendShutdownSignal to PID '%d': %w", process.Pid, e)
    29	        }
    30	
    31	        return nil
    32	}
    33	
    34	func sysProcAttrs() *syscall.SysProcAttr {
    35	        // By default, a ctrl-break event applies to a whole process group, which ends up
    36	        // shutting down the supervisor. Instead, we spawn the collector in its own process
    37	        // group, so that sending a ctrl-break event shuts down just the collector.
    38	        return &syscall.SysProcAttr{
    39	                CreationFlags: syscall.CREATE_NEW_PROCESS_GROUP,
    40	        }
    41	}
    42

    85	type configState struct {
    86	        // Supervisor-assembled config to be given to the Collector.
    87	        mergedConfig string
    88	        // true if the server provided configmap was empty
    89	        configMapIsEmpty bool
    90	}

    92	func (c *configState) equal(other *configState) bool {
    93	        return other.mergedConfig == c.mergedConfig && other.configMapIsEmpty == c.configMapIsEmpty
    94	}

   107	
   108	// Supervisor implements supervising of OpenTelemetry Collector and uses OpAMPClient
   109	// to work with an OpAMP Server.
   110	type Supervisor struct {
   111	        pidProvider pidProvider
   112	
   113	        // Commander that starts/stops the Agent process.
   114	        commander *commander.Commander
   115	
   116	        startedAt time.Time
   117	
   118	        // Supervisor's own config.
   119	        config config.Supervisor
   120	
   121	        agentDescription    *atomic.Value
   122	        availableComponents *atomic.Value
   123	
   124	        // Supervisor's persistent state
   125	        persistentState *persistentState
   126	
   127	        noopPipelineTemplate   *template.Template
   128	        opampextensionTemplate *template.Template
   129	        extraConfigTemplate    *template.Template
   130	        ownTelemetryTemplate   *template.Template
   131	
   132	        agentConn *atomic.Value
   133	
   134	        // A config section to be added to the Collector's config to fetch its own metrics.
   135	        // TODO: store this persistently so that when starting we can compose the effective
   136	        // config correctly.
   137	        // https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector-contrib/issues/21078
   138	        agentConfigOwnMetricsSection *atomic.Value
   139	
   140	        // Internal config state for agent use. See the [configState] struct for more details.
   141	        cfgState *atomic.Value
   142	
   143	        // Final effective config of the Collector.
   144	        effectiveConfig *atomic.Value
   145	
   146	        // Last received remote config.
   147	        remoteConfig *protobufs.AgentRemoteConfig
   148	
   149	        // A channel to indicate there is a new config to apply.
   150	        hasNewConfig chan struct{}
   151	        // configApplyTimeout is the maximum time to wait for the agent to apply a new config.
   152	        // After this time passes without the agent reporting health as OK, the agent is considered unhealthy.
   153	        configApplyTimeout time.Duration
   154	        // lastHealthFromClient is the last health status of the agent received from the client.
   155	        lastHealthFromClient atomic.Pointer[protobufs.ComponentHealth]
   156	
   157	        // The OpAMP client to connect to the OpAMP Server.
   158	        opampClient client.OpAMPClient
   159	
   160	        doneChan chan struct{}
   161	        agentWG  sync.WaitGroup
   162	
   163	        customMessageToServer chan *protobufs.CustomMessage
   164	        customMessageWG       sync.WaitGroup
   165	
   166	        // agentHasStarted is true if the agent has started.
   167	        agentHasStarted bool
   168	        // agentStartHealthCheckAttempts is the number of health check attempts made by the agent since it started.
   169	        agentStartHealthCheckAttempts int
   170	        // agentRestarting is true if the agent is restarting.
   171	        agentRestarting atomic.Bool
   172	
   173	        // The OpAMP server to communicate with the Collector's OpAMP extension
   174	        opampServer     server.OpAMPServer
   175	        opampServerPort int
   176	
   177	        telemetrySettings telemetrySettings
   178	
   179	        featureGates map[string]struct{}
   180	}
   181	
   182	func NewSupervisor(logger *zap.Logger, cfg config.Supervisor) (*Supervisor, error) {
   183	        s := &Supervisor{
   184	                pidProvider:                  defaultPIDProvider{},
   185	                hasNewConfig:                 make(chan struct{}, 1),
   186	                agentConfigOwnMetricsSection: &atomic.Value{},
   187	                cfgState:                     &atomic.Value{},
   188	                effectiveConfig:              &atomic.Value{},
   189	                agentDescription:             &atomic.Value{},
   190	                availableComponents:          &atomic.Value{},
   191	                doneChan:                     make(chan struct{}),
   192	                customMessageToServer:        make(chan *protobufs.CustomMessage, maxBufferedCustomMessages),
   193	                agentConn:                    &atomic.Value{},
   194	                featureGates:                 map[string]struct{}{},
   195	        }
   196	        if err := s.createTemplates(); err != nil {
   197	                return nil, err
   198	        }
   199	
   200	        telSettings, err := initTelemetrySettings(logger, cfg.Telemetry)
   201	        if err != nil {
   202	                return nil, err
   203	        }
   204	        s.telemetrySettings = telSettings
   205	
   206	        if err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {
   207	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error validating config: %w", err)
   208	        }
   209	        s.config = cfg
   210	
   211	        if err := os.MkdirAll(s.config.Storage.Directory, 0o700); err != nil {
   212	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error creating storage dir: %w", err)
   213	        }
   214	
   215	        s.configApplyTimeout = s.config.Agent.ConfigApplyTimeout
   216	
   217	        return s, nil
   218	}
   219	
   220	func initTelemetrySettings(logger *zap.Logger, cfg config.Telemetry) (telemetrySettings, error) {
   221	        readers := cfg.Metrics.Readers
   222	        if cfg.Metrics.Level == configtelemetry.LevelNone {
   223	                readers = []telemetryconfig.MetricReader{}
   224	        }
   225	
   226	        pcommonRes := pcommon.NewResource()
   227	        for k, v := range cfg.Resource {
   228	                pcommonRes.Attributes().PutStr(k, *v)
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        if _, ok := cfg.Resource[string(semconv.ServiceNameKey)]; !ok {
   232	                pcommonRes.Attributes().PutStr(string(semconv.ServiceNameKey), "opamp-supervisor")
   233	        }
   234	
   235	        if _, ok := cfg.Resource[string(semconv.ServiceInstanceIDKey)]; !ok {
   236	                instanceUUID, _ := uuid.NewRandom()
   237	                instanceID := instanceUUID.String()
   238	                pcommonRes.Attributes().PutStr(string(semconv.ServiceInstanceIDKey), instanceID)
   239	        }
   240	
   241	        // TODO currently we do not have the build info containing the version available to set semconv.ServiceVersionKey
   242	
   243	        var attrs []telemetryconfig.AttributeNameValue
   244	        for k, v := range pcommonRes.Attributes().All() {
   245	                attrs = append(attrs, telemetryconfig.AttributeNameValue{Name: k, Value: v.Str()})
   246	        }
   247	
   248	        sch := semconv.SchemaURL
   249	
   250	        ctx := context.Background()
   251	
   252	        sdk, err := telemetryconfig.NewSDK(
   253	                telemetryconfig.WithContext(ctx),
   254	                telemetryconfig.WithOpenTelemetryConfiguration(
   255	                        telemetryconfig.OpenTelemetryConfiguration{
   256	                                MeterProvider: &telemetryconfig.MeterProvider{
   257	                                        Readers: readers,
   258	                                },
   259	                                TracerProvider: &telemetryconfig.TracerProvider{
   260	                                        Processors: cfg.Traces.Processors,
   261	                                },
   262	                                LoggerProvider: &telemetryconfig.LoggerProvider{
   263	                                        Processors: cfg.Logs.Processors,
   264	                                },
   265	                                Resource: &telemetryconfig.Resource{
   266	                                        SchemaUrl:  &sch,
   267	                                        Attributes: attrs,
   268	                                },
   269	                        },
   270	                ),
   271	        )
   272	        if err != nil {
   273	                return telemetrySettings{}, err
   274	        }
   275	
   276	        var lp log.LoggerProvider
   277	        if len(cfg.Logs.Processors) > 0 {
   278	                lp = sdk.LoggerProvider()
   279	                logger = logger.WithOptions(zap.WrapCore(func(c zapcore.Core) zapcore.Core {
   280	                        core, err := zapcore.NewIncreaseLevelCore(zapcore.NewTee(
   281	                                c,
   282	                                otelzap.NewCore("github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector-contrib/cmd/opampsupervisor",
   283	                                        otelzap.WithLoggerProvider(lp),
   284	                                ),
   285	                        ), zap.NewAtomicLevelAt(cfg.Logs.Level))
   286	                        if err != nil {
   287	                                panic(err)
   288	                        }
   289	                        return core
   290	                }))
   291	        }
   292	
   293	        return telemetrySettings{
   294	                component.TelemetrySettings{
   295	                        Logger:         logger,
   296	                        TracerProvider: sdk.TracerProvider(),
   297	                        MeterProvider:  sdk.MeterProvider(),
   298	                        Resource:       pcommonRes,
   299	                },
   300	                lp,
   301	        }, nil
   302	}
   303	
   304	func (s *Supervisor) Start() error {
   305	        var err error
   306	        s.persistentState, err = loadOrCreatePersistentState(s.persistentStateFilePath(), s.telemetrySettings.Logger)
   307	        if err != nil {
   308	                return err
   309	        }
   310	
   311	        if err = s.getFeatureGates(); err != nil {
   312	                return fmt.Errorf("could not get feature gates from the Collector: %w", err)
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        if err = s.getBootstrapInfo(); err != nil {
   316	                return fmt.Errorf("could not get bootstrap info from the Collector: %w", err)
   317	        }
   318	
   319	        s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Info("Supervisor starting",
   320	                zap.String("id", s.persistentState.InstanceID.String()))
   321	
   322	        if err = s.startOpAMP(); err != nil {
   323	                return fmt.Errorf("cannot start OpAMP client: %w", err)
   324	        }
   325	
   326	        err = s.loadAndWriteInitialMergedConfig()
   327	        if err != nil {
   328	                return fmt.Errorf("failed loading initial config: %w", err)
   329	        }
   330	
   331	        s.commander, err = commander.NewCommander(
   332	                s.telemetrySettings.Logger,
   333	                s.config.Storage.Directory,
   334	                s.config.Agent,
   335	                "--config", s.agentConfigFilePath(),
   336	        )
   337	        if err != nil {
   338	                return err
   339	        }
   340	
   341	        s.agentWG.Add(1)
   342	        go func() {
   343	                defer s.agentWG.Done()
   344	                s.runAgentProcess()
   345	        }()
   346	
   347	        s.customMessageWG.Add(1)
   348	        go func() {
   349	                defer s.customMessageWG.Done()
   350	                s.forwardCustomMessagesToServerLoop()
   351	        }()
   352	
   353	        return nil
   354	}
   355	
   356	func (s *Supervisor) getFeatureGates() error {
   357	        cmd, err := commander.NewCommander(
   358	                s.telemetrySettings.Logger,
   359	                s.config.Storage.Directory,
   360	                s.config.Agent,
   361	                "featuregate",
   362	        )
   363	        if err != nil {
   364	                return err
   365	        }
   366	
   367	        stdout, _, err := cmd.StartOneShot()
   368	        if err != nil {
   369	                return err
   370	        }
   371	        scanner := bufio.NewScanner(bytes.NewBuffer(stdout))
   372	
   373	        // First line only contains headers, discard it.
   374	        _ = scanner.Scan()
   375	        for scanner.Scan() {
   376	                line := scanner.Text()
   377	                i := strings.Index(line, " ")
   378	                flag := line[0:i]
   379	
   380	                if flag == AllowNoPipelinesFeatureGate {
   381	                        s.featureGates[AllowNoPipelinesFeatureGate] = struct{}{}
   382	                }
   383	        }
   384	        if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
   385	                fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, "reading standard input:", err)
   386	        }
   387	
   388	        return nil
   389	}
   390	
   391	func (s *Supervisor) createTemplates() error {
   392	        var err error
   393	
   394	        if s.noopPipelineTemplate, err = template.New("nooppipeline").Parse(noopPipelineTpl); err != nil {
   395	                return err
   396	        }
   397	        if s.extraConfigTemplate, err = template.New("extraconfig").Parse(extraConfigTpl); err != nil {
   398	                return err
   399	        }
   400	        if s.opampextensionTemplate, err = template.New("opampextension").Parse(opampextensionTpl); err != nil {
   401	                return err
   402	        }
   403	        if s.ownTelemetryTemplate, err = template.New("owntelemetry").Parse(ownTelemetryTpl); err != nil {
   404	                return err
   405	        }
   406	
   407	        return nil
   408	}
   409	
   410	// getBootstrapInfo obtains the Collector's agent description by
   411	// starting a Collector with a specific config that only starts
   412	// an OpAMP extension, obtains the agent description, then
   413	// shuts down the Collector. This only needs to happen
   414	// once per Collector binary.
   415	func (s *Supervisor) getBootstrapInfo() (err error) {
   416	        _, span := s.getTracer().Start(context.Background(), "GetBootstrapInfo")
   417	        defer span.End()
   418	        s.opampServerPort, err = s.getSupervisorOpAMPServerPort()
   419	        if err != nil {
   420	                span.SetStatus(codes.Error, fmt.Sprintf("Could not get supervisor opamp service port: %v", err))
   421	                return err
   422	        }
   423	
   424	        bootstrapConfig, err := s.composeNoopConfig()
   425	        if err != nil {
   426	                span.SetStatus(codes.Error, fmt.Sprintf("Could not compose noop config config: %v", err))
   427	                return err
   428	        }
   429	
   430	        err = os.WriteFile(s.agentConfigFilePath(), bootstrapConfig, 0o600)
   431	        if err != nil {
   432	                span.SetStatus(codes.Error, fmt.Sprintf("Failed to write agent config: %v", err))
   433	                return fmt.Errorf("failed to write agent config: %w", err)
   434	        }
   435	
   436	        srv := server.New(newLoggerFromZap(s.telemetrySettings.Logger, "opamp-server"))
   437	
   438	        done := make(chan error, 1)
   439	        var connected atomic.Bool
   440	        var doneReported atomic.Bool
   441	
   442	        // Start a one-shot server to get the Collector's agent description
   443	        // and available components using the Collector's OpAMP extension.
   444	        err = srv.Start(flattenedSettings{
   445	                endpoint: fmt.Sprintf("localhost:%d", s.opampServerPort),
   446	                onConnecting: func(_ *http.Request) (bool, int) {
   447	                        connected.Store(true)
   448	                        return true, http.StatusOK
   449	                },
   450	                onMessage: func(_ serverTypes.Connection, message *protobufs.AgentToServer) *protobufs.ServerToAgent {
   451	                        response := &protobufs.ServerToAgent{}
   452	                        if message.GetAvailableComponents() != nil {
   453	                                s.setAvailableComponents(message.AvailableComponents)
   454	                        }
   455	
   456	                        if message.AgentDescription != nil {
   457	                                instanceIDSeen := false
   458	                                s.setAgentDescription(message.AgentDescription)
   459	                                identAttr := message.AgentDescription.IdentifyingAttributes
   460	
   461	                                for _, attr := range identAttr {
   462	                                        if attr.Key == string(semconv.ServiceInstanceIDKey) {
   463	                                                if attr.Value.GetStringValue() != s.persistentState.InstanceID.String() {
   464	                                                        done <- fmt.Errorf(
   465	                                                                "the Collector's instance ID (%s) does not match with the instance ID set by the Supervisor (%s): %w",
   466	                                                                attr.Value.GetStringValue(),
   467	                                                                s.persistentState.InstanceID.String(),
   468	                                                                errNonMatchingInstanceUID,
   469	                                                        )
   470	                                                        return response
   471	                                                }
   472	                                                instanceIDSeen = true
   473	                                        }
   474	                                }
   475	
   476	                                if !instanceIDSeen {
   477	                                        done <- errors.New("the Collector did not specify an instance ID in its AgentDescription message")
   478	                                        return response
   479	                                }
   480	                        }
   481	
   482	                        // agent description must be defined
   483	                        _, ok := s.agentDescription.Load().(*protobufs.AgentDescription)
   484	                        if !ok {
   485	                                return response
   486	                        }
   487	
   488	                        // if available components have not been reported, agent description is sufficient to continue
   489	                        availableComponents, availableComponentsOk := s.availableComponents.Load().(*protobufs.AvailableComponents)
   490	                        if availableComponentsOk {
   491	                                // must have a full list of components if available components have been reported
   492	                                if availableComponents.GetComponents() != nil {
   493	                                        if !doneReported.Load() {
   494	                                                done <- nil
   495	                                                doneReported.Store(true)
   496	                                        }
   497	                                } else {
   498	                                        // if we don't have a full component list, ask for it
   499	                                        response.Flags = uint64(protobufs.ServerToAgentFlags_ServerToAgentFlags_ReportAvailableComponents)
   500	                                }
   501	                                return response
   502	                        }
   503	
   504	                        // need to only report done once, not on each message - otherwise, we get a hung thread
   505	                        if !doneReported.Load() {
   506	                                done <- nil
   507	                                doneReported.Store(true)
   508	                        }
   509	
   510	                        return response
   511	                },
   512	        }.toServerSettings())
   513	        if err != nil {
   514	                span.SetStatus(codes.Error, fmt.Sprintf("Could not start OpAMP server: %v", err))
   515	                return err
   516	        }
   517	
   518	        defer func() {
   519	                if stopErr := srv.Stop(context.Background()); stopErr != nil {
   520	                        err = errors.Join(err, fmt.Errorf("error when stopping the opamp server: %w", stopErr))
   521	                }
   522	        }()
   523	
   524	        flags := []string{
   525	                "--config", s.agentConfigFilePath(),
   526	        }
   527	        featuregateFlag := s.getFeatureGateFlag()
   528	        if len(featuregateFlag) > 0 {
   529	                flags = append(flags, featuregateFlag...)
   530	        }
   531	        cmd, err := commander.NewCommander(
   532	                s.telemetrySettings.Logger,
   533	                s.config.Storage.Directory,
   534	                s.config.Agent,
   535	                flags...,
   536	        )
   537	        if err != nil {
   538	                span.SetStatus(codes.Error, fmt.Sprintf("Could not start Agent: %v", err))
   539	                return err
   540	        }
   541

  1442	func (s *Supervisor) stopAgentApplyConfig() {

  1302	func (s *Supervisor) startAgent() (agentStartStatus, error) {
  1303	        if s.cfgState.Load().(*configState).configMapIsEmpty {
  1304	                // Don't start the agent if there is no config to run
  1305	                s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Info("No config present, not starting agent.")
  1306	                // need to manually trigger updating effective config
  1307	                err := s.opampClient.UpdateEffectiveConfig(context.Background())
  1308	                if err != nil {
  1309	                        s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Error("The OpAMP client failed to update the effective config", zap.Error(err))
  1310	                }
  1311	                return agentNotStarting, nil
  1312	        }
  1313	
  1314	        err := s.commander.Start(context.Background())
  1315	        if err != nil {
  1316	                s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Error("Cannot start the agent", zap.Error(err))
  1317	                startErr := fmt.Errorf("cannot start the agent: %w", err)
  1318	                err = s.opampClient.SetHealth(&protobufs.ComponentHealth{Healthy: false, LastError: startErr.Error()})
  1319	                if err != nil {
  1320	                        s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Error("Failed to report OpAMP client health", zap.Error(err))
  1321	                }
  1322	                return "", startErr
  1323	        }
  1324	
  1325	        s.agentHasStarted = false
  1326	        s.agentStartHealthCheckAttempts = 0
  1327	        s.startedAt = time.Now()
  1328	
  1329	        return agentStarting, nil
  1330	}

    25	        "go.uber.org/zap/zapcore"
    26	)
    27	
    28	// Supervisor is the Supervisor config file format.
    29	type Supervisor struct {
    30	        Server       OpAMPServer  `mapstructure:"server"`
    31	        Agent        Agent        `mapstructure:"agent"`
    32	        Capabilities Capabilities `mapstructure:"capabilities"`
    33	        Storage      Storage      `mapstructure:"storage"`
    34	        Telemetry    Telemetry    `mapstructure:"telemetry"`
    35	}
    36	
    37	// Load loads the Supervisor config from a file.
    38	func Load(configFile string) (Supervisor, error) {
    39	        if configFile == "" {
    40	                return Supervisor{}, errors.New("path to config file cannot be empty")
    41	        }
    42	
    43	        resolverSettings := confmap.ResolverSettings{
    44	                URIs: []string{configFile},
    45	                ProviderFactories: []confmap.ProviderFactory{
    46	                        fileprovider.NewFactory(),
    47	                        envprovider.NewFactory(),
    48	                },
    49	                ConverterFactories: []confmap.ConverterFactory{},
    50	                DefaultScheme:      "env",
    51	        }
    52	
    53	        resolver, err := confmap.NewResolver(resolverSettings)
    54	        if err != nil {
    55	                return Supervisor{}, err
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        conf, err := resolver.Resolve(context.Background())
    59	        if err != nil {
    60	                return Supervisor{}, err
    61	        }
    62	
    63	        cfg := DefaultSupervisor()
    64	        if err = conf.Unmarshal(&cfg); err != nil {
    65	                return Supervisor{}, err
    66	        }
    67	
    68	        if err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {
    69	                return Supervisor{}, fmt.Errorf("cannot validate supervisor config %s: %w", configFile, err)
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        return cfg, nil
    73	}
    74	
    75	func (s Supervisor) Validate() error {
    76	        if err := s.Server.Validate(); err != nil {
    77	                return err
    78	        }
    79	
    80	        if err := s.Agent.Validate(); err != nil {
    81	                return err
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        return nil
    85	}
    86	
    87	type Storage struct {
    88	        // Directory is the directory where the Supervisor will store its data.
    89	        Directory string `mapstructure:"directory"`
    90	}
    91	
    92	// Capabilities is the set of capabilities that the Supervisor supports.
    93	type Capabilities struct {
    94	        AcceptsRemoteConfig            bool `mapstructure:"accepts_remote_config"`
    95	        AcceptsRestartCommand          bool `mapstructure:"accepts_restart_command"`
    96	        AcceptsOpAMPConnectionSettings bool `mapstructure:"accepts_opamp_connection_settings"`
    97	        ReportsEffectiveConfig         bool `mapstructure:"reports_effective_config"`
    98	        ReportsOwnMetrics              bool `mapstructure:"reports_own_metrics"`
    99	        ReportsOwnLogs                 bool `mapstructure:"reports_own_logs"`
   100	        ReportsOwnTraces               bool `mapstructure:"reports_own_traces"`
   101	        ReportsHealth                  bool `mapstructure:"reports_health"`
   102	        ReportsRemoteConfig            bool `mapstructure:"reports_remote_config"`
   103	        ReportsAvailableComponents     bool `mapstructure:"reports_available_components"`
   104	}
   105	
   106	func (c Capabilities) SupportedCapabilities() protobufs.AgentCapabilities {
   107	        supportedCapabilities := protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_ReportsStatus
   108	
   109	        if c.ReportsEffectiveConfig {
   110	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_ReportsEffectiveConfig
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        if c.ReportsHealth {
   114	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_ReportsHealth
   115	        }
   116	
   117	        if c.ReportsOwnMetrics {
   118	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_ReportsOwnMetrics
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        if c.ReportsOwnLogs {
   122	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_ReportsOwnLogs
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        if c.ReportsOwnTraces {
   126	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_ReportsOwnTraces
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        if c.AcceptsRemoteConfig {
   130	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_AcceptsRemoteConfig
   131	        }
   132	
   133	        if c.ReportsRemoteConfig {
   134	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_ReportsRemoteConfig
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        if c.AcceptsRestartCommand {
   138	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_AcceptsRestartCommand
   139	        }
   140	
   141	        if c.AcceptsOpAMPConnectionSettings {
   142	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_AcceptsOpAMPConnectionSettings
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        if c.ReportsAvailableComponents {
   146	                supportedCapabilities |= protobufs.AgentCapabilities_AgentCapabilities_ReportsAvailableComponents
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        return supportedCapabilities
   150	}
   151	
   152	type OpAMPServer struct {
   153	        Endpoint string                 `mapstructure:"endpoint"`
   154	        Headers  http.Header            `mapstructure:"headers"`
   155	        TLS      configtls.ClientConfig `mapstructure:"tls,omitempty"`
   156	}
   157	
   158	func (o OpAMPServer) Validate() error {
   159	        if o.Endpoint == "" {
   160	                return errors.New("server::endpoint must be specified")
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        url, err := url.Parse(o.Endpoint)
   164	        if err != nil {
   165	                return fmt.Errorf("invalid URL for server::endpoint: %w", err)
   166	        }
   167	
   168	        switch url.Scheme {
   169	        case "http", "https", "ws", "wss":
   170	        default:
   171	                return fmt.Errorf(`invalid scheme %q for server::endpoint, must be one of "http", "https", "ws", or "wss"`, url.Scheme)
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        err = o.TLS.Validate()
   175	        if err != nil {
   176	                return fmt.Errorf("invalid server::tls settings: %w", err)
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        return nil
   180	}
   181	
   182	type Agent struct {
   183	        Executable              string            `mapstructure:"executable"`
   184	        OrphanDetectionInterval time.Duration     `mapstructure:"orphan_detection_interval"`
   185	        Description             AgentDescription  `mapstructure:"description"`
   186	        ConfigApplyTimeout      time.Duration     `mapstructure:"config_apply_timeout"`
   187	        BootstrapTimeout        time.Duration     `mapstructure:"bootstrap_timeout"`
   188	        OpAMPServerPort         int               `mapstructure:"opamp_server_port"`
   189	        PassthroughLogs         bool              `mapstructure:"passthrough_logs"`
   190	        ConfigFiles             []string          `mapstructure:"config_files"`
   191	        Arguments               []string          `mapstructure:"args"`
   192	        Env                     map[string]string `mapstructure:"env"`
   193	}
   194	
   195	func (a Agent) Validate() error {
   196	        if a.OrphanDetectionInterval <= 0 {
   197	                return errors.New("agent::orphan_detection_interval must be positive")
   198	        }
   199	
   200	        if a.BootstrapTimeout <= 0 {
   201	                return errors.New("agent::bootstrap_timeout must be positive")
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        if a.OpAMPServerPort < 0 || a.OpAMPServerPort > 65535 {
   205	                return errors.New("agent::opamp_server_port must be a valid port number")
   206	        }
   207	
   208	        if a.Executable == "" {
   209	                return errors.New("agent::executable must be specified")
   210	        }
   211	
   212	        _, err := os.Stat(a.Executable)
   213	        if err != nil {
   214	                return fmt.Errorf("could not stat agent::executable path: %w", err)
   215	        }
   216	
   217	        if a.ConfigApplyTimeout <= 0 {
   218	                return errors.New("agent::config_apply_timeout must be valid duration")
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        return nil
   222	}
   223	
   224	type AgentDescription struct {
   225	        IdentifyingAttributes    map[string]string `mapstructure:"identifying_attributes"`
   226	        NonIdentifyingAttributes map[string]string `mapstructure:"non_identifying_attributes"`
   227	}
   228	
   229	type Telemetry struct {
   230	        // TODO: Add more telemetry options
   231	        // Issue here: https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-collector-contrib/issues/35582
   232	        Logs    Logs                   `mapstructure:"logs"`
   233	        Metrics Metrics                `mapstructure:"metrics"`
   234	        Traces  telemetry.TracesConfig `mapstructure:"traces"`
   235	
   236	        Resource map[string]*string `mapstructure:"resource"`
   237	}
   238	
   239	type Logs struct {
   240	        Level            zapcore.Level `mapstructure:"level"`
   241	        ErrorOutputPaths []string      `mapstructure:"error_output_paths"`
   242	        OutputPaths      []string      `mapstructure:"output_paths"`
   243	        // Processors allow configuration of log record processors to emit logs to
   244	        // any number of supported backends.
   245	        Processors []config.LogRecordProcessor `mapstructure:"processors,omitempty"`
   246	}
   247	
   248	type Metrics struct {
   249	        Level   configtelemetry.Level `mapstructure:"level"`
   250	        Readers []config.MetricReader `mapstructure:"readers"`
   251	}
   252	
   253	// DefaultSupervisor returns the default supervisor config
   254	func DefaultSupervisor() Supervisor {
   255	        defaultStorageDir := "/var/lib/otelcol/supervisor"
   256	        if runtime.GOOS == "windows" {
   257	                // Windows default is "%ProgramData%\Otelcol\Supervisor"
   258	                // If the ProgramData environment variable is not set,
   259	                // it falls back to C:\ProgramData
   260	                programDataDir := os.Getenv("ProgramData")
   261	                if programDataDir == "" {
   262	                        programDataDir = `C:\ProgramData`
   263	                }
   264	
   265	                defaultStorageDir = filepath.Join(programDataDir, "Otelcol", "Supervisor")
   266	        }
   267	
   268	        return Supervisor{
   269	                Capabilities: Capabilities{
   270	                        AcceptsRemoteConfig:            false,
   271	                        AcceptsRestartCommand:          false,
   272	                        AcceptsOpAMPConnectionSettings: false,
   273	                        ReportsEffectiveConfig:         true,
   274	                        ReportsOwnMetrics:              true,
   275	                        ReportsOwnLogs:                 false,
   276	                        ReportsOwnTraces:               false,
   277	                        ReportsHealth:                  true,
   278	                        ReportsRemoteConfig:            false,
   279	                        ReportsAvailableComponents:     false,
   280	                },
   281	                Storage: Storage{
   282	                        Directory: defaultStorageDir,
   283	                },
   284	                Agent: Agent{
   285	                        OrphanDetectionInterval: 5 * time.Second,
   286	                        ConfigApplyTimeout:      5 * time.Second,
   287	                        BootstrapTimeout:        3 * time.Second,
   288	                        PassthroughLogs:         false,
   289	                },
   290	                Telemetry: Telemetry{
   291	                        Logs: Logs{
   292	                                Level:            zapcore.InfoLevel,
   293	                                OutputPaths:      []string{"stdout"},
   294	                                ErrorOutputPaths: []string{"stderr"},
   295	                        },
   296	                },
   297	        }
   298	}
   299

cat <<EOF > reproduce_issue.go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"os/exec"
	"syscall"
	"time"
)

func main() {
	// Simple collector mock that handles SIGHUP
	mockCollectorSource := \`
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"os/signal"
	"syscall"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Collector started")
	sigCh := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
	signal.Notify(sigCh, syscall.SIGHUP, syscall.SIGTERM, syscall.SIGINT)

	for {
		sig := <-sigCh
		fmt.Printf("Received signal: %s\n", sig)
		if sig == syscall.SIGHUP {
			fmt.Println("Reloading configuration...")
		} else {
			fmt.Println("Exiting...")
			os.Exit(0)
		}
	}
}
\`
	os.WriteFile("mock_collector.go", []byte(mockCollectorSource), 0644)
	exec.Command("go", "build", "-o", "mock_collector", "mock_collector.go").Run()
	defer os.Remove("mock_collector")
	defer os.Remove("mock_collector.go")

	fmt.Println("Starting mock collector...")
	cmd := exec.Command("./mock_collector")
	stdout, _ := cmd.StdoutPipe()
	cmd.Start()

	go func() {
		buf := make([]byte, 1024)
		for {
			n, err := stdout.Read(buf)
			if n > 0 {
				fmt.Print(string(buf[:n]))
			}
			if err != nil {
				break
			}
		}
	}()

	time.Sleep(1 * time.Second)
	fmt.Println("Sending SIGHUP to mock collector...")
	cmd.Process.Signal(syscall.SIGHUP)
	time.Sleep(1 * time.Second)

	fmt.Println("Sending SIGTERM to mock collector...")
	cmd.Process.Signal(syscall.SIGTERM)
	cmd.Wait()
}
EOF

package main

import (
	"context"

	"os/exec"
	"syscall"
	"time"
)

func main() {
	// Simple collector mock that handles SIGHUP
	mockCollectorSource := \`
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"os/signal"
	"syscall"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Collector started")
	sigCh := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
	signal.Notify(sigCh, syscall.SIGHUP, syscall.SIGTERM, syscall.SIGINT)

	for {
		sig := <-sigCh
		fmt.Printf("Received signal: %s\n", sig)
		if sig == syscall.SIGHUP {
			fmt.Println("Reloading configuration...")
		} else {
			fmt.Println("Exiting...")
			os.Exit(0)
		}
	}
}
\`
	os.WriteFile("mock_collector.go", []byte(mockCollectorSource), 0644)
	exec.Command("go", "build", "-o", "mock_collector", "mock_collector.go").Run()
	defer os.Remove("mock_collector")
	defer os.Remove("mock_collector.go")

	fmt.Println("Starting mock collector...")
	cmd := exec.Command("./mock_collector")
	stdout, _ := cmd.StdoutPipe()
	cmd.Start()

	go func() {
		buf := make([]byte, 1024)
		for {
			n, err := stdout.Read(buf)
			if n > 0 {
				fmt.Print(string(buf[:n]))
			}
			if err != nil {
				break
			}
		}
	}()

	time.Sleep(1 * time.Second)
	fmt.Println("Sending SIGHUP to mock collector...")
	cmd.Process.Signal(syscall.SIGHUP)
	time.Sleep(1 * time.Second)

	fmt.Println("Sending SIGTERM to mock collector...")
	cmd.Process.Signal(syscall.SIGTERM)
	cmd.Wait()
}

🎬 ACTION
cat <<'EOF' > reproduce_issue.go
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"os/exec"
	"syscall"
	"time"
)

func main() {
	// Simple collector mock that handles SIGHUP
	mockCollectorSource := `
package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"os/signal"
	"syscall"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Collector started")
	sigCh := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
	signal.Notify(sigCh, syscall.SIGHUP, syscall.SIGTERM, syscall.SIGINT)

	for {
		sig := <-sigCh
		fmt.Printf("Received signal: %s\n", sig)
		if sig == syscall.SIGHUP {
			fmt.Println("Reloading configuration...")
		} else {
			fmt.Println("Exiting...")
			os.Exit(0)
		}
	}
}
`
	os.WriteFile("mock_collector.go", []byte(mockCollectorSource), 0644)
	exec.Command("go", "build", "-o", "mock_collector", "mock_collector.go").Run()
	defer os.Remove("mock_collector")
	defer os.Remove("mock_collector.go")

	fmt.Println("Starting mock collector...")
	cmd := exec.Command("./mock_collector")
	stdout, _ := cmd.StdoutPipe()
	cmd.Start()

	go func() {
		buf := make([]byte, 1024)
		for {
			n, err := stdout.Read(buf)
			if n > 0 {
				fmt.Print(string(buf[:n]))
			}
			if err != nil {
				break
			}
		}
	}()

	time.Sleep(1 * time.Second)
	fmt.Println("Sending SIGHUP to mock collector...")
	cmd.Process.Signal(syscall.SIGHUP)
	time.Sleep(1 * time.Second)

	fmt.Println("Sending SIGTERM to mock collector...")
	cmd.Process.Signal(syscall.SIGTERM)
	cmd.Wait()
}
EOF
go run reproduce_issue.go

+        cmd.Env = common.EnvVarMapToEnvMapSlice(c.cfg.Env)
+        cmd.SysProcAttr = sysProcAttrs()
+        // grab cmd pipes
+        stdoutPipe, err := cmd.StdoutPipe()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("stdoutPipe: %w", err)
+        }
+        stderrPipe, err := cmd.StderrPipe()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("stderrPipe: %w", err)
+        }
+
+        // start agent
+        if err := cmd.Start(); err != nil {
+                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("start: %w", err)
+        }
+        // capture agent output
+        go func() {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stdoutPipe)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        stdout = append(stdout, scanner.Bytes()...)
+                        stdout = append(stdout, byte('\n'))
+                }
+                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
+                        c.logger.Error("Error reading agent stdout: %w", zap.Error(err))
+                }
+        }()
+        go func() {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stderrPipe)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        stderr = append(stderr, scanner.Bytes()...)
+                        stderr = append(stderr, byte('\n'))
+                }
+                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
+                        c.logger.Error("Error reading agent stderr: %w", zap.Error(err))
+                }
+        }()
+
+        c.logger.Debug("Agent process started", zap.Int("pid", cmd.Process.Pid))
+
+        doneCh := make(chan struct{}, 1)
+
+        go func() {
+                err := cmd.Wait()
+                if err != nil {
+                        c.logger.Error("One-shot Collector encountered an error during execution", zap.Error(err))
+                }
+                doneCh <- struct{}{}
+        }()
+
+        waitCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 3*time.Second)
+
+        defer cancel()
+
+        select {
+        case <-doneCh:
+        case <-waitCtx.Done():
+                pid := cmd.Process.Pid
+                c.logger.Debug("Stopping agent process", zap.Int("pid", pid))
+
+                // Gracefully signal process to stop.
+                if err := sendShutdownSignal(cmd.Process); err != nil {
+                        return nil, nil, err
+                }
+
+                innerWaitCtx, innerCancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 10*time.Second)
+
+                // Setup a goroutine to wait a while for process to finish and send kill signal
+                // to the process if it doesn't finish.
+                var innerErr error
+                go func() {
+                        <-innerWaitCtx.Done()
+
+                        if !errors.Is(innerWaitCtx.Err(), context.DeadlineExceeded) {
+                                c.logger.Debug("Agent process successfully stopped.", zap.Int("pid", pid))
+                                return
+                        }
+
+                        // Time is out. Kill the process.
+                        c.logger.Debug(
+                                "Agent process is not responding to SIGTERM. Sending SIGKILL to kill forcibly.",
+                                zap.Int("pid", pid))
+                        if innerErr = cmd.Process.Signal(os.Kill); innerErr != nil {
+                                return
+                        }
+                }()
+
+                innerCancel()
+        }
+
+        return stdout, stderr, nil
 }

 // and if the process does not finish kills it forcedly by sending SIGKILL.

+        if c.running.Load() == 0 {

+

+        <-c.doneCh

+        c.running.Store(0)

+        cancel()

+        return innerErr

 func sysProcAttrs() *syscall.SysProcAttr {

+        if configFile == "" {
+                return Supervisor{}, errors.New("path to config file cannot be empty")
+        }
+
+        resolverSettings := confmap.ResolverSettings{
+                URIs: []string{configFile},
+                ProviderFactories: []confmap.ProviderFactory{
+                        fileprovider.NewFactory(),
+                        envprovider.NewFactory(),
+                },
+                ConverterFactories: []confmap.ConverterFactory{},
+                DefaultScheme:      "env",
+        }
+
+        resolver, err := confmap.NewResolver(resolverSettings)
+        if err != nil {
+                return Supervisor{}, err
+        }
+
+        conf, err := resolver.Resolve(context.Background())
+        if err != nil {
+                return Supervisor{}, err
+        }
+
+        cfg := DefaultSupervisor()
+        if err = conf.Unmarshal(&cfg); err != nil {
+                return Supervisor{}, err
+        }
+
+        if err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {
+                return Supervisor{}, fmt.Errorf("cannot validate supervisor config %s: %w", configFile, err)
+        }
+
+        return cfg, nil
 }

+        // cmd.Wait returns an exec.ExitError when the Collector exits unsuccessfully or stops
+        // after receiving a signal. The Commander caller will handle these cases, so we filter
+        // them out here.
+        var exitError *exec.ExitError
+        if ok := errors.As(err, &exitError); err != nil && !ok {
+                c.logger.Error("An error occurred while watching the agent process", zap.Error(err))
+        }
+

+        c.doneCh <- struct{}{}

+        cmd := exec.CommandContext(ctx, c.cfg.Executable, c.args...) // #nosec G204
+        cmd.Env = common.EnvVarMapToEnvMapSlice(c.cfg.Env)
+        cmd.SysProcAttr = sysProcAttrs()
+        // grab cmd pipes
+        stdoutPipe, err := cmd.StdoutPipe()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("stdoutPipe: %w", err)
+        }
+        stderrPipe, err := cmd.StderrPipe()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("stderrPipe: %w", err)
+        }
+
+        // start agent
+        if err := cmd.Start(); err != nil {
+                return nil, nil, fmt.Errorf("start: %w", err)
+        }
+        // capture agent output
+        go func() {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stdoutPipe)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        stdout = append(stdout, scanner.Bytes()...)
+                        stdout = append(stdout, byte('\n'))
+                }
+                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
+                        c.logger.Error("Error reading agent stdout: %w", zap.Error(err))
+                }
+        }()
+        go func() {
+                scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stderrPipe)
+                for scanner.Scan() {
+                        stderr = append(stderr, scanner.Bytes()...)
+                        stderr = append(stderr, byte('\n'))
+                }
+                if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
+                        c.logger.Error("Error reading agent stderr: %w", zap.Error(err))
+                }

+        c.logger.Debug("Agent process started", zap.Int("pid", cmd.Process.Pid))

+        doneCh := make(chan struct{}, 1)
+
+        go func() {
+                err := cmd.Wait()
+                if err != nil {
+                        c.logger.Error("One-shot Collector encountered an error during execution", zap.Error(err))
+                }
+                doneCh <- struct{}{}
+        }()
+
+        waitCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 3*time.Second)
+
+        defer cancel()
+
+        select {
+        case <-doneCh:
+        case <-waitCtx.Done():
+                pid := cmd.Process.Pid
+                c.logger.Debug("Stopping agent process", zap.Int("pid", pid))
+
+                // Gracefully signal process to stop.
+                if err := sendShutdownSignal(cmd.Process); err != nil {
+                        return nil, nil, err
+                }
+
+                innerWaitCtx, innerCancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 10*time.Second)
+
+                // Setup a goroutine to wait a while for process to finish and send kill signal
+                // to the process if it doesn't finish.
+                var innerErr error
+                go func() {
+                        <-innerWaitCtx.Done()
+
+                        if !errors.Is(innerWaitCtx.Err(), context.DeadlineExceeded) {
+                                c.logger.Debug("Agent process successfully stopped.", zap.Int("pid", pid))
+                                return
+                        }
+
+                        // Time is out. Kill the process.
+                        c.logger.Debug(
+                                "Agent process is not responding to SIGTERM. Sending SIGKILL to kill forcibly.",
+                                zap.Int("pid", pid))
+                        if innerErr = cmd.Process.Signal(os.Kill); innerErr != nil {
+                                return
+                        }
+                }()
+
+                innerCancel()
+        }
+
+        return stdout, stderr, nil

 // Stop the Agent process. Sends SIGTERM to the process and wait for up 10 seconds
 // and if the process does not finish kills it forcedly by sending SIGKILL.
 // Returns after the process is terminated.
 func (c *Commander) Stop(ctx context.Context) error {

+        if c.running.Load() == 0 {
+                // Not started, nothing to do.
+                return nil
+        }
+
+        pid := c.cmd.Process.Pid
+        c.logger.Debug("Stopping agent process", zap.Int("pid", pid))
+
+        // Gracefully signal process to stop.
+        if err := sendShutdownSignal(c.cmd.Process); err != nil {
+                return err
+        }
+
+        waitCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, 10*time.Second)
+
+        // Setup a goroutine to wait a while for process to finish and send kill signal
+        // to the process if it doesn't finish.
+        var innerErr error
+        go func() {
+                <-waitCtx.Done()
+
+                if !errors.Is(waitCtx.Err(), context.DeadlineExceeded) {
+                        c.logger.Debug("Agent process successfully stopped.", zap.Int("pid", pid))
+                        return
+                }
+
+                // Time is out. Kill the process.
+                c.logger.Debug(
+                        "Agent process is not responding to SIGTERM. Sending SIGKILL to kill forcibly.",
+                        zap.Int("pid", pid))
+                if innerErr = c.cmd.Process.Signal(os.Kill); innerErr != nil {
+                        return
+                }
+        }()
+
+        // Wait for process to terminate
+        <-c.doneCh
+
+        c.running.Store(0)
+
+        // Let goroutine know process is finished.
+        cancel()
+
+        return innerErr
 }
+
+func (c *Commander) Reload(ctx context.Context) error {
+if c.running.Load() == 0 {
+return c.Start(ctx)
+}
+
+c.logger.Debug("Reloading agent", zap.String("agent", c.cfg.Executable))
+return sendReloadSignal(c.cmd.Process)
+}

+                s.config.Storage.Directory,
+                s.config.Agent,
+                "featuregate",

+        _ = scanner.Scan()
+        for scanner.Scan() {
+                line := scanner.Text()
+                i := strings.Index(line, " ")
+                flag := line[0:i]
+
+                if flag == AllowNoPipelinesFeatureGate {
+                        s.featureGates[AllowNoPipelinesFeatureGate] = struct{}{}
+                }
+        }
+        if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {

+        // and available components using the Collector's OpAMP extension.

+                onConnecting: func(_ *http.Request) (bool, int) {
+                        connected.Store(true)
+                        return true, http.StatusOK

+                onMessage: func(_ serverTypes.Connection, message *protobufs.AgentToServer) *protobufs.ServerToAgent {
+                        response := &protobufs.ServerToAgent{}
+                        if message.GetAvailableComponents() != nil {
+                                s.setAvailableComponents(message.AvailableComponents)
+                        }
+
+                        if message.AgentDescription != nil {
+                                instanceIDSeen := false
+                                s.setAgentDescription(message.AgentDescription)
+                                identAttr := message.AgentDescription.IdentifyingAttributes
+

+                                        if attr.Key == string(semconv.ServiceInstanceIDKey) {
+                                                if attr.Value.GetStringValue() != s.persistentState.InstanceID.String() {
+                                                        done <- fmt.Errorf(
+                                                                "the Collector's instance ID (%s) does not match with the instance ID set by the Supervisor (%s): %w",
+                                                                attr.Value.GetStringValue(),
+                                                                s.persistentState.InstanceID.String(),
+                                                                errNonMatchingInstanceUID,
+                                                        )
+                                                        return response
+                                                }
+                                                instanceIDSeen = true
+                                        }
+                                }
+
+                                if !instanceIDSeen {
+                                        done <- errors.New("the Collector did not specify an instance ID in its AgentDescription message")
+                                        return response
+                                }
+                        }
+
+                        // agent description must be defined
+                        _, ok := s.agentDescription.Load().(*protobufs.AgentDescription)
+                        if !ok {
+                                return response
+                        }
+
+                        // if available components have not been reported, agent description is sufficient to continue
+                        availableComponents, availableComponentsOk := s.availableComponents.Load().(*protobufs.AvailableComponents)
+                        if availableComponentsOk {
+                                // must have a full list of components if available components have been reported
+                                if availableComponents.GetComponents() != nil {
+                                        if !doneReported.Load() {
+                                                done <- nil
+                                                doneReported.Store(true)
+                                        }
+                                } else {
+                                        // if we don't have a full component list, ask for it
+                                        response.Flags = uint64(protobufs.ServerToAgentFlags_ServerToAgentFlags_ReportAvailableComponents)
+                                }
+                                return response
+                        }
+
+                        // need to only report done once, not on each message - otherwise, we get a hung thread
+                        if !doneReported.Load() {
+                                done <- nil
+                                doneReported.Store(true)
+                        }
+
+                        return response
+                },
+        }.toServerSettings())
+        if err != nil {
+                span.SetStatus(codes.Error, fmt.Sprintf("Could not start OpAMP server: %v", err))
+                return err
+        }
+
+        defer func() {
+                if stopErr := srv.Stop(context.Background()); stopErr != nil {
+                        err = errors.Join(err, fmt.Errorf("error when stopping the opamp server: %w", stopErr))
+                }
+        }()
+
+        flags := []string{
+                "--config", s.agentConfigFilePath(),
+        }
+        featuregateFlag := s.getFeatureGateFlag()
+        if len(featuregateFlag) > 0 {
+                flags = append(flags, featuregateFlag...)

+        cmd, err := commander.NewCommander(
+                s.telemetrySettings.Logger,
+                s.config.Storage.Directory,
+                s.config.Agent,
+                flags...,
+        )
+        if err != nil {
+                span.SetStatus(codes.Error, fmt.Sprintf("Could not start Agent: %v", err))
+                return err
+        }
+
+        if err = cmd.Start(context.Background()); err != nil {
+                span.SetStatus(codes.Error, fmt.Sprintf("Could not start Agent: %v", err))
+                return err
+        }
+
+        defer func() {
+                if stopErr := cmd.Stop(context.Background()); stopErr != nil {
+                        err = errors.Join(err, fmt.Errorf("error when stopping the collector: %w", stopErr))
+                }
+        }()
+
+        select {
+        case <-time.After(s.config.Agent.BootstrapTimeout):
+                if connected.Load() {
+                        msg := "collector connected but never responded with an AgentDescription message"
+                        span.SetStatus(codes.Error, msg)
+                        return errors.New(msg)
+                } else {
+                        msg := "collector's OpAMP client never connected to the Supervisor"
+                        span.SetStatus(codes.Error, msg)
+                        return errors.New(msg)
+                }
+        case err = <-done:
+                if errors.Is(err, errNonMatchingInstanceUID) {
+                        // try to report the issue to the OpAMP server
+                        if startOpAMPErr := s.startOpAMPClient(); startOpAMPErr == nil {
+                                defer func(s *Supervisor) {
+                                        if stopErr := s.stopOpAMPClient(); stopErr != nil {
+                                                s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Error("Could not stop OpAmp client", zap.Error(stopErr))
+                                        }
+                                }(s)
+                                if healthErr := s.opampClient.SetHealth(&protobufs.ComponentHealth{
+                                        Healthy:   false,
+                                        LastError: err.Error(),
+                                }); healthErr != nil {
+                                        s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Error("Could not report health to OpAMP server", zap.Error(healthErr))
+                                }
+                        } else {
+                                s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Error("Could not start OpAMP client to report health to server", zap.Error(startOpAMPErr))
+                        }
+                }
+                if err != nil {
+                        s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Error("Could not complete bootstrap", zap.Error(err))
+                        span.SetStatus(codes.Error, err.Error())
+                } else {
+                        span.SetStatus(codes.Ok, "")
+                }

 // applyKeyValueOverrides merges the overrides map into the array of key value pairs.
 // If a key from overrides already exists in the array of key value pairs, it is overwritten by the value from the overrides map.
 // An array of KeyValue pair is returned, with each key value pair having a distinct key.
 func applyKeyValueOverrides(overrides map[string]string, orig []*protobufs.KeyValue) []*protobufs.KeyValue {
-	kvMap := make(map[string]*protobufs.KeyValue, len(orig)+len(overrides))
-
-	for _, kv := range orig {
-		kvMap[kv.Key] = kv
-	}
-
-	for k, v := range overrides {
-		kvMap[k] = &protobufs.KeyValue{
-			Key: k,
-			Value: &protobufs.AnyValue{
-				Value: &protobufs.AnyValue_StringValue{
-					StringValue: v,
-				},
-			},
-		}
-	}
-
-	// Sort keys for stable output, makes it easier to test.
-	keys := make([]string, 0, len(kvMap))
-	for k := range kvMap {
-		keys = append(keys, k)
-	}
-
-	sort.Strings(keys)
-
-	kvOut := make([]*protobufs.KeyValue, 0, len(kvMap))
-	for _, k := range keys {
-		v := kvMap[k]
-		kvOut = append(kvOut, v)
-	}
-
-	return kvOut
+        kvMap := make(map[string]*protobufs.KeyValue, len(orig)+len(overrides))
+
+        for _, kv := range orig {
+                kvMap[kv.Key] = kv
+        }
+
+        for k, v := range overrides {
+                kvMap[k] = &protobufs.KeyValue{
+                        Key: k,
+                        Value: &protobufs.AnyValue{
+                                Value: &protobufs.AnyValue_StringValue{
+                                        StringValue: v,
+                                },
+                        },
+                }
+        }
+
+        // Sort keys for stable output, makes it easier to test.
+        keys := make([]string, 0, len(kvMap))
+        for k := range kvMap {
+                keys = append(keys, k)
+        }
+
+        sort.Strings(keys)
+
+        kvOut := make([]*protobufs.KeyValue, 0, len(kvMap))
+        for _, k := range keys {
+                v := kvMap[k]
+                kvOut = append(kvOut, v)
+        }
+
+        return kvOut
 }

-		// revert the OpAMP server config

-		// start the OpAMP client with the old settings
-		if err := s.startOpAMPClient(); err != nil {
-			s.telemetrySettings.Logger.Error("Cannot reconnect to the OpAMP server after restoring old settings", zap.Error(err))
